Guard is always very friendly and their instructions are always concise and helpful. We did have a fuel tank busted on a reefer that was on this yard, but we cannot be certain it happened on site. This is the best business I've been to in La Jolla! The owner is super friendly and always  personally offering samples of yogurt he changes frequently to keep it amazing and interesting. It is far better than a self serve place for sanitary reasons and to make it feel like a friendly, family owned stop. We love the interior, with high ceiling,  and my daughter and her friend counted nearly 40 decorative frogs in the place for fun. We come here 2-3 times after a class. The owner even makes me any type of coffee I want that's not on the menu, like Mexican mocha coffee or ghirardelli chocolate coffee, or even kona coffee yogurt iced coffee! We were here 2 years ago and the owner even remembered us. Now he's making frozen yogurt pies and maybe frozen yogurt cakes next that will sure to be a hit as ice cream cakes tend to soften too slowly! Can't wait! Thank you, Froglanders!!<//review>

< text>
I had been searching for a mid size SUV when I came across a listing for
a Chevy Equinox at, Affordable Kars. After test driving a few cars in my area, I decided to drive out to Affordable Kars with my mechanic to have a closer look at the Equinox.
We showed up to the lot without an appointment and were greeted by Sylvia and Jose. They were both friendly, personable and very knowledgeable about all the cars on their lot. I liked a few of the cars they had but I was really there for the Equinox.
After a test drive and quick inspection, my mechanic assured me it was a good car and that I should buy it. So i did.
I drive the car daily and take frequent trips to the desert with it. I've called Affordable Kars a few times over the past year for advice on small things like oil changes etc.. and they are always there to assist me.
I purchased my car from Affordable Kars in 2019 and all I can say is, this was a great buy.
Id like to give a big Thank You shoutout to Affordable Kars, Sylvia and Jose for an awesome, stress free, used car buying experience.

No answer at all.  Never mind the fact that when I finally had the product in my hand, it said "solvent free."  It would be more practical to run a place with people who know how to answer simple questions about the product they are selling.  And it's a bit on the pricey side: like Las Vegas prices.  Also, a message on the door about "closing it behind you when you leave," on the way out is not practical.
